They first came for the Catholics, 
but I was a Protestant, so did nothing.

Then they came for the Communists,
but I wasn‚Äôt a communist, so I did nothing.

Then they came for the trade unionists,
but I wasn‚Äôt a trade unionist, so I did nothing.

Then they came for the Jews,
but I wasn‚Äôt a Jew, so I did nothing.

By the time they came for me,
there was nobody to speak up.

Martin Niemoller (1892-1984)
